delete\n  IF TG_OP = 'DELETE' THEN\n    UPDATE categories\n    SET product_count = product_count - 1\n    WHERE id = OLD.category_id;\n  END IF;\n  \n  RETURN NEW;\nEND;\n$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;\n\n-- Create trigger\nDROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS trigger_update_category_count ON products;\nCREATE TRIGGER trigger_update_category_count\nAFTER INSERT OR UPDATE OR DELETE ON products\nFOR EACH ROW\nEXECUTE FUNCTION update_category_count_on_product_change();\n\n-- Initial product count update\nSELECT update_category_product_counts();\n\n-- Note: You may need to manually update existing products to link them to categories\n-- Example:\n-- UPDATE products SET category_id = '1' WHERE category ILIKE '%electronics%';\n-- UPDATE products SET category_id = '2' WHERE category ILIKE '%home%' OR category ILIKE '%kitchen%';\n-- etc.\n",

Fast)\n\n**Run this SQL** in Supabase SQL Editor:\n\n```sql\n-- Link products by matching category name\nUPDATE products SET category_id = '1' WHERE category ILIKE '%electronic%';\nUPDATE products SET category_id = '2' WHERE category ILIKE '%home%' OR category ILIKE '%kitchen%';\nUPDATE products SET category_id = '3' WHERE category ILIKE '%fashion%' OR category ILIKE '%apparel%';\nUPDATE products SET category_id = '4' WHERE category ILIKE '%beauty%' OR category ILIKE '%personal care%';\nUPDATE products SET category_id = '5' WHERE category ILIKE '%health%' OR category ILIKE '%wellness%';\nUPDATE products SET category_id = '9' WHERE category ILIKE '%pet%';\nUPDATE products SET category_id = '16' WHERE category ILIKE '%gam%';\nUPDATE products SET category_id = '17' WHERE category ILIKE '%smart home%';\nUPDATE products SET category_id = '23' WHERE category ILIKE '%phone%';\nUPDATE products SET category_id = '24' WHERE category ILIKE '%computer%' OR category ILIKE '%laptop%';\nUPDATE products SET category_id = '25' WHERE category ILIKE '%audio%' OR category ILIKE '%headphone%';\n```\n\nThis automatically links products based on their old category field!\n\n---\n\n## \ud83c\udfa8 COLOR SCHEME REFERENCE\n\n**FomoGeo Brand Colors:**\n\n- **Primary (Emerald)**: #10B981\n- **Secondary (Slate)**: #0F172A\n- **Accent (Amber)**: #F59E0B -
